		}

		bypass = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { country_exists = LIT }
				NOT = { country_exists = LAT }
				NOT = { country_exists = EST }
			}
		}

		prerequisite = { focus = BLR_new_democratic_constituon	}

		ai_will_do = { factor = 10
		}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BLR_baltic_economic_cooperation"

				limit = {
					country_exists = LIT
					NOT = { has_war_with = BLR }
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = LIT
					modifier = trade_mission
				}
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = LIT
					modifier = trade_mission
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = LAT
					NOT = { has_war_with = BLR }
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = LAT
					modifier = trade_mission
				}
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = LAT

				}
			}

					add_idea = partial_draft_army
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = volunteer_army }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = volunteer_army
					add_idea = partial_draft_army
				}
			}

				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = draft_army
					add_idea = partial_draft_army
				}
			}
			block_conscription_change = yes
		}

				name = "Tatiana  Golubeva"

					emerging_Communist-State

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BLR_connect_to_neighbours"
			every_neighbor_country = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						emerging_communist_state_are_in_power = yes
					}

					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = ROOT
						modifier = POL_comm_connection_big
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = ROOT
						modifier = POL_comm_connection_small
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		icon = attack_estonia

		x = 2
		y = 7

		relative_position_id = BLR_reestablish_the_military_industrial_complex

		ai_will_do = { factor = 20 }

		available = {
			EST = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = { has_war_with = BLR }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = BLR }
			}
			emerging_communist_state_are_in_power = yes
		}

		bypass = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = EST }
					is_in_faction_with = EST
					has_war_with = EST
				}
			}
		cancel = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = EST }
					is_in_faction_with = EST
					has_war_with = EST
				}
			}

		prerequisite = { focus = BLR_soviet_legacy }

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BLR_estonia_problem"

	focus = {
		id = BLR_promoting_unity
		icon = blr_accounting_chamber

		x = -1
		y = 1

		relative_position_id = BLR_start

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 90
		}

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }

		cost = 7

		bypass = {
			is_subject = yes
			has_autonomy_state = autonomy_union_state
		}

		prerequisite = { focus = BLR_start }

		available = {
			SOV = { has_government = communism }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = UNS_support_for_union_more_40
				check_variable = { BLR.union_state > 40 }
			}
			is_subject = no
			has_idea = BLR_union_integration_part1

		}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BLR_promoting_unity"
			add_stability = 0.09
